<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的表格基础模型（TabPFN 2.5）缺乏对其内部计算机制的深入理解。研究者旨在通过因果分析，探究该模型如何跨层分配计算，以及其注意力头在特征层面的运作方式。

Method: 采用了因果机制分析方法，具体包括：1. 激活修补（Activation Patching）；2. 消融实验（Ablation）；3. 注意力熵分析（Attention Entropy）；4. 对比激活引导（Contrastive Activation Steering）。实验基于两个合成回归数据集进行。

Result: 研究发现：1. 存在显著的时间专业化现象，即存在一个主导注意力头，其因果必要性在峰值层比其他头高出2到5倍；2. 该主导头的活跃层位置随任务复杂度动态变化；3. 其余头部表现出对称的后期层配置；4. 基于对比激活的推理引导在样本间迁移失败，验证了其通过动态语境注意力而非固定参数方向进行上下文学习的本质。

Conclusion: 本研究通过因果机制分析揭示了TabPFN 2.5在处理表格数据时的计算特性。研究指出，该模型通过语境依赖的注意力机制编码任务结构，而非像大语言模型那样依赖稳定的参数方向，这解释了为什么基于激活的对比引导在TabPFN中难以跨样本迁移。

Abstract: We present the first causal mechanistic analysis of a tabular foundation model, investigating how TabPFN 2.5's feature wise attention heads distribute computation across layers. Using activation patching, ablation, and attention entropy across two synthetic regression datasets, we find clear temporal specialisation: one head's causal necessity dominates that of the others by 2 to 5 times at peak layer, with its dominant layer shifting across tasks of different complexity, while the remaining heads exhibit symmetric late layer profiles. Attention entropy and patching provide convergent evidence for the computationally active layers of the dominant head. We additionally investigate inference time steerability via contrastive activation steering, which fails to transfer across samples. We attribute this result to TabPFN's in context learning mechanism, which encodes task structure through context dependent attention rather than the stable parametric directions that make steering tractable in language models.

</details>


### [125] [LoRA-Muon: Spectral Steepest Descent on the Low-Rank Manifold](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12921)
*Franz Louis Cesista,Katherine Crowson,Cédric Simal,Stella Biderman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 LoRA-Muon，这是一种基于谱最速下降法的低秩微调优化器，解决了传统 LoRA 对超参数敏感和性能受限的问题，实现了极佳的学习率迁移性和超越全秩训练的性能，且计算更加高效友好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管 LoRA 显著降低了计算和内存需求，但其在微调过程中存在超参数调优困难、对初始化敏感、学习率难以在不同秩之间迁移，且性能往往难以超越全秩（dense）训练基线的问题。因此，需要一种更稳健、更易于调优的低秩优化算法。

Method: 本文提出了 LoRA-Muon 优化器，通过将 Muon 优化器的谱最速下降（spectral steepest-descent）规则应用于低秩（LoRA）设置，并引入了“拆分权重衰减”（split weight-decay）规则。该方法避免了 QR 分解，无需存储二阶矩信息，从而提高了在硬件上的执行效率。

Result: 实验表明，LoRA-Muon 的最优学习率可以在不同的秩、宽度、深度和因子缩放之间稳定迁移。在 TinyShakespeare 的基准测试中，Rank-2 的 LoRA-Muon 能够达到全秩训练的最优水平，而 Rank-32 的版本在种子平均评估中表现优于全秩基线。相比 Spectron 和 LoRA-RITE，LoRA-Muon 在计算效率和内存占用上更具优势。

Conclusion: LoRA-Muon 是一种高效的低秩微调优化器，它通过应用谱最速下降规则，成功解决了传统 LoRA 在超参数敏感性、学习率迁移性以及性能上限方面的瓶颈，能够作为全秩优化器的有效低秩代理，且在硬件加速和内存效率上表现优异。

Abstract: Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) significantly reduces compute and memory costs for finetuning Deep Learning models but is often harder to tune than dense training: when using factor-wise optimizers such as AdamW, it is sensitive to initialization choices, its optimal learning rates transfer poorly across ranks, and it often fails to beat dense baselines. We derive LoRA-Muon by applying the Muon optimizer's spectral steepest-descent rule to the low-rank setting. Along with our split weight-decay rule, our main claim is that LoRA-Muon is a good low-rank proxy for full-rank Muon and Shampoo-family optimizers. Its optimal learning rates transfer across rank, width, depth, and factor-rescaling. In our compute-matched TinyShakespeare study, a rank-$2$ proxy recovers the dense best tested learning rate, and a rank-$32$ LoRA-Muon run attains lower mean validation loss than the dense baseline in the seed-averaged sweep. We further show that the Spectron optimizer depends on arbitrary factor scaling, so it would likely be a poor fit when finetuning starts from badly imbalanced factors, and that LoRA-RITE's simplified QR-coordinate core implements the same spectral update. LoRA-Muon computes that update without QR-decomposition and avoids storing second moments, making it more accelerator-friendly and memory-efficient.

</details>


### [126] [Order Is Not Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12923)
*Gareth Seneque,Lap-Hang Ho,Nafise Erfanian Saeedi,Jeffrey Molendijk,Tim Elson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文挑战了将“秩序”等同于“控制”的观念，提出了一种基于受体门控的响应定律，通过对生物神经系统和LLM的定量分析，揭示了控制在介观尺度下的物理本质与局限，证明了系统响应具有高度的可预测性和算子结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI对齐、可解释性和神经扰动研究往往将“秩序”（order）等同于“控制”（control），但在定义控制的本质及其物理机制上存在缺失。作者旨在通过建立一种更严谨、基于物理的控制理论，明确控制在生物系统和AI系统中的具体表现形式与限制。

Method: 研究采用了跨学科的分析框架，综合了神经生物学（小鼠ALM、秀丽隐杆线虫、斑马鱼）的实验数据与大语言模型（LLM）的实证分析。通过引入“受体门控响应定律”（receiver-gated response law），构建了映射材料状态、驱动、浴槽与受体状态的算子，利用组件符号准确率、系统效应预测准确率等指标验证了响应的可预测性。

Result: 研究发现LLM的生成输出遵循可预测的响应规律：在四种材料条件下，响应向量的组件符号准确率达到72.8%-73.7%（非零组件达84.3%-84.8%）；系统效应和目标家族的预测准确率分别达到93.6%和91.7%。实验证明，控制是局部的、受介质和受体状态约束的，且能够通过有限努力实现目标类别的移动。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于驱动-耗散响应系统的介观控制理论。结论指出，控制并非简单的“秩序”，而是存在于物理和LLM中的局部响应规律。该模型成功界定了控制的边界（如饱和、超速、损耗），并证明了响应算子具有可预测性，从而为理解AI系统与生物系统的控制机理提供了定量框架。

Abstract: AI alignment, interpretability, steering, and neural perturbation studies identify order-inducing objects. We argue that order is not control. Control requires a receiver-gated response law: a denominator-indexed operator mapping material state, action/drive, bath, and receiver state to response displacement, sinks, effort, and basin projection. We identify it across biological, LLM, adapter, and stochastic-operator panels. The laws are local: an intervention can be admitted, saturated, sign-changing, leaky, or overdriven depending on medium, bath, receiver state, action port, and comparator. Control is assigned when finite effort moves a target or outcome-readout class under the same denominator while damage, null/evasive, invalid format, overdrive, and unnecessary effort stay bounded. Mouse ALM, C. elegans, and zebrafish panels provide physical response-operator evidence while excluding coordinate identity and controller conclusions. LLM panels show generated-output response laws: across four material conditions, response vectors are predictable at 72.8-73.7% component-sign accuracy, rising to 84.3-84.8% on nonzero components; held-out observers predict system-effect and target/oracle families at 93.6% and 91.7% accuracy. Constitution-conditioned adapters reshape susceptibility as prepared media, and stochastic-operator panels separate measured opportunity from deployable action policies. This gives a driven-dissipative response-system account at the mesoscopic control level: drives act through prepared media, baths, and receivers, producing admitted movement, impedance, sinks, or overdrive. The evidence supports local admitted control and measurable stochastic response operators, while leaving deployable pre-generation control, hidden/logit causal sufficiency, biological-to-LLM coordinate identity, and literal thermodynamic quantities outside scope.

### [127] [Is Spurious Correlation Removal Always Learnable?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12930)
*Yibo Zhou,Bo Li,Hai-Miao Hu,Hanzi Wang,Xiaokang Zhang,Ruifan Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了不变学习中存在的“计算复杂性壁垒”，证明了在统计可识别的情形下，多项式时间内仍可能无法学习不变特征。文章通过环境多样性参数 $\gamma$ 量化了学习难度，并推导了样本复杂度的相变临界点，为评估不变学习算法的局限性提供了理论基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管不变学习在理论上是可识别的，但在实际应用中仍面临失效风险。研究旨在揭示这种失效背后的计算性质，探讨在什么条件下计算复杂性会阻碍不变特征的恢复，并定量分析环境多样性对学习难度和误差界限的影响。

Method: 1. 理论建模：引入基于黑盒可采样监督稀疏恢复原语的条件计算复杂性分析；
2. 复杂性证明：构建多环境实例，证明在特定假设下，尽管存在可被穷举搜索学习的解，但不存在多项式时间的恢复算法；
3. 统计分析：引入分离参数γ量化环境多样性，并结合局部高斯正则性推导极大极小风险（minimax risk）；
4. 相变分析：研究在标签诱导偏移下的学习误差扩展与样本复杂度相变点；
5. 实证验证：使用合成数据集和真实数据集验证理论预测的性能差距和相变现象。

Result: 1. 证明了在黑盒稀疏恢复原语下，存在多项式时间内无法解决的不变学习问题；
2. 推导出不变子空间估计的极大极小风险误差公式 $\mathbb{E}[\text{dist}(\hat{V},V_{\text{inv}})^2] = \Theta(k(d-k)/(n|\mathcal{E}|))$；
3. 发现了在标签诱导偏移下，算法性能在样本复杂度 $n^* \propto k(d-k)/(|\mathcal{E}|\gamma^2)$ 处发生相变，且误差与环境多样性参数 $\gamma^2$ 成反比。

Conclusion: 不变学习存在本质的计算复杂性壁垒。即使在统计上可识别的情况下，有效的恢复算法可能在多项式时间内无法找到不变子空间。此外，环境多样性（参数γ）是决定学习难度和收敛速度的关键因素，当多样性不足或存在标签诱导的偏移时，学习性能会发生显著的相变。

Abstract: Invariant learning can fail even when the invariant structure is statistically identifiable. We show a conditional computational barrier: under a black-box samplable supervised sparse recovery primitive motivated by average-case sparse-recovery reductions, there exist \emph{samplable} multi-environment instances with a one-dimensional predictive invariant subspace ($k=1$) that are learnable with polynomial samples by exhaustive search, while any polynomial-time constant-accuracy recovery algorithm would contradict the primitive. We further quantify environment diversity by a separation parameter $γ$, which controls identifiability and the curvature of invariance objectives. Under sufficient diversity and local Gaussian regularity, the minimax risk is $\mathbb{E}[\dist(\hat{V},V_{\mathrm{inv}})^2]=Θ(k(d-k)/(n|\mathcal{E}|))$, and under label-induced shifts a phase transition occurs at $n^*\propto k(d-k)/(|\mathcal{E}|γ^2)$ with refined estimation error scaling proportional to $1/γ^2$. Synthetic and real datasets illustrate the predicted gaps and transitions and motivate simple diversity diagnostics.

</details>


### [128] [Circuit Synchronization Precedes Generalization: Causal Evidence from Fourier Structure in Grokking Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12966)
*Achyuthan Sivasankar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文引入频率同步度（FSD）作为Grokking现象的早期预测指标，通过因果干预实验证明了Grokking的延迟期由正则化决定，且该现象依赖于多层Transformer架构的傅里叶电路同步。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 提出频率同步度（FSD）指标，用于无需预设知识即可量化傅里叶电路的同步过程；2. 在九种模块化加法配置下进行实验，对比FSD与损失函数表现；3. 通过在FSD峰值处分叉训练并改变权重衰减系数（lambda），进行因果干预实验；4. 对不同模型架构（注意力机制、MLP、单层模型）进行消融实验。

Result: 1. FSD是目前已知的最早预测Grokking的指标，通常比现象发生提前约1722步；2. 发现Grokking的延迟期本质上是一种正则化现象，且延迟时间与权重衰减系数呈反比关系（Delta_t ~ C/lambda）；3. 证实了该机制依赖于多层网络架构，而非单层网络或纯MLP结构。

Conclusion: 研究确立了傅里叶电路同步与Grokking现象的因果关系，证实了正则化强度直接调控中间阶段的时长，并揭示了该机制依赖于多层架构的特性。

Abstract: Grokking -- where a transformer on modular arithmetic suddenly transitions from near-chance to near-perfect validation accuracy -- is attributed to a Fourier circuit, but its timing, causal structure, and controllability remain poorly understood. We introduce the Frequency Synchronization Degree (FSD), a normalised, permutation-tested metric for Fourier circuit synchronisation requiring no prior circuit knowledge. Across nine modular addition configurations (primes p in {53, 71, 97, 113, 131}, three seeds), FSD synchronises 500-3,000 steps before grokking (mean lead +1,722 steps; all nine positive, sign-test p~0.004), and precedes a restricted-logit loss baseline (Nanda et al.'s excluded loss) in all nine cases, making it the earliest available predictor. We provide direct causal evidence that the inter-phase gap is a regularisation phenomenon: forking training at the FSD-ceiling step and varying weight decay lambda produces strictly monotone earlier grokking, with Delta_t proportional to 1/lambda. This law replicates across three primes (p in {53,97,131}; R^2=1.00 and R^2=0.99 for two clean cases), captured as Delta_t ~ C/lambda, consistent with (1/lambda)*log(||W_mem||/tau). Architecture ablations show an attention-only model groks with a strong FSD precursor; an MLP-only model never groks; a single-layer model's FSD lags, confirming the precursor is a multi-block circuit property.

Abstract: Estimating cognitive load from speech has largely been studied in controlled laboratory settings, with limited understanding of its reliability in natural collaborative conversations. Results show conversational interaction provides useful signals for predicting cognitive load related to time pressure, mental work, effort, and task performance. ### [130] [EPM-JEPA: Operator-Side Experience Modulation in JEPA-Family World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12979)
*Vedant Pandya*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了如何在JEPA世界模型中通过经验回放应对分布偏移。通过对比两种机制，发现基于LoRA的权重调制（EPM-JEPA）优于隐藏状态注入，并指出此类模型性能受限于多种动力学过程，而非简单的收敛，从而提出了物理导向的改进方案。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究对比了两种将积累经验纳入JEPA预测器的机制：1. 算子侧调制（EPM-JEPA）：利用经验表征通过LoRA技术在预测器权重中生成低秩权重增量；2. 操作数侧注入（EI-JEPA）：将压缩后的经验表征作为残差添加到预测器的隐藏状态中。并在Moving MNIST重力偏移任务中进行了预注册比较。

Conclusion: 研究发现，基于权重调制的EPM-JEPA在处理分布偏移时优于基于状态注入的EI-JEPA。同时，该研究揭示了此类动态预测模型中存在三种独立的动力学过程（缓冲循环、EMA目标漂移及LoRA固有的瞬态响应），而非模型已收敛至稳态。这些发现直接催生了物理感知模型PEM-JEPA。

Abstract: JEPA-family world models use a static predictor whose weights do not adapt when test-time dynamics diverge from training. We compare two mechanisms for incorporating accumulated experience into a JEPA predictor under distribution shift: operand-side injection, where a compressed experience representation is added as a residual to the predictor's hidden state (EI-JEPA), and operator-side modulation, where the same representation generates low-rank weight deltas via LoRA applied to the predictor's weights (EPM-JEPA). On a pre-registered comparison (Moving MNIST, gravity shift), EPM-JEPA (D_shift^{n=50} = 0.7848 +/- 0.0078, three seeds) differs from EI-JEPA (0.8238) by delta = 4.74% - Outcome C: a null result - by our stated criterion, a valid outcome. As a secondary, non-pre-registered observation, EPM-JEPA improves 1.90% over a no-memory baseline (0.8000), consistently across seeds, while EI-JEPA underperforms the baseline, indicating the benefit is specific to weight-level modulation. Our primary contribution is a mechanism analysis: the D_shift^{n=50} trajectory reflects three independent dynamical processes - buffer cycling, EMA target drift, and an intrinsic LoRA settling transient of +0.021 - rather than convergence to equilibrium. These findings motivate PEM-JEPA, a physics-grounded successor addressing this dynamical-peak limitation.

### [131] [Exposure Bias as Epistemic Underidentification in Recursive Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12990)
*Riku Green,Zahraa S. Abdallah,Telmo M Silva Filho*

TL;DR: 该论文指出多步递归预测的难点不仅在于分布偏移，更源于因模型对自生成状态缺乏认知而导致的“认知不确定性”，并提出了基于溯源变量的分析与修正框架。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多步递归预测通常被解释为简单的分布偏移问题，但该解释在处理部分可观测或状态截断情况时是不完整的，作者旨在揭示递归滚动预测中潜在的认知不确定性及其对模型性能的影响。

Method: 提出了一种形式化框架，通过引入诱导状态（induced states $Z$）和溯源变量（provenance variables $P$）来分析递归预测；将诱导状态误差分解为教师强制/滚动预测不匹配、表示类近似以及溯源信息缺口；并通过实证分析验证了滚动预测进入了独特的诱导状态区间。

Result: 证明了即使在确定性潜在动力学下，单步监督也无法充分识别递归预测所需的局部目标；实证结果显示，滚动预测会引导模型进入独特的诱导状态区间；通过引入溯源感知修正，可以进一步缓解上述问题带来的性能损失。

Conclusion: 研究表明，“暴露偏差”（exposure bias）的本质不仅是分布偏移，更是一种在自诱导认知不确定性下的推理问题。通过将误差分解并引入溯源变量，论文明确了递归预测在多步预测中面临的状态空间重构难题。

Abstract: Recursive multi-step forecasting is usually framed as distribution shift: models are trained on observed histories but deployed on their own predictions. We show this framing is incomplete by proving that, under partial observability or state truncation, recursive rollout is also an epistemic underidentification problem. Even with deterministic latent dynamics, one-step Bayes supervision identifies behavior only on observed contexts and need not identify the deployed recursive predictor once rollout queries self-generated induced states whose correct local targets are not determined by numeric state alone. We formalize this with induced states $Z$ and provenance variables $P$, and derive a decomposition of induced-state error into teacher-forcing/rollout mismatch, representation--class approximation, and provenance information gaps. Empirically, we show that rollout enters a distinct induced-state regime, that fixed induced states define a distinct local corrective task, and that closed-loop gains arise not only from local adaptation but also from changing the induced states visited during rollout. Using a simple binary provenance encoding, provenance-aware correction can further improve performance, though gains are conditional rather than uniform. These results recast exposure bias as reasoning under self-induced epistemic uncertainty.

</details>


### [132] [DeepJEB++: Foundation Model-Driven Large-Scale 3D Engineering Dataset via 2D Latent Space Augmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12994)
*Soyoung Yoo,Leekyo Jeong,Jinsu Ra,Dongeon Lee,Sunwoong Yang,Hyogu Jeong,Namwoo Kang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DeepJEB++ 是一种通过 2D 潜在空间增强并自动标注的框架，解决了工程领域高质量 3D 数据集稀缺的问题，实现了低资源消耗下的 40 倍数据规模扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前数据驱动的工程设计受到大规模 3D 物理性能标注数据集匮乏的限制，且现有的 3D 数据增强技术难以在保持几何多样性的同时实现自动化仿真标注。

Method: 提出了一种三阶段框架：首先，利用预训练的 2D 潜在扩散模型进行多视图合成与潜在插值，并结合视觉语言模型（VLM）进行质量过滤；其次，通过领域自适应生成模型将 2D 图像提升为 3D 网格；最后，通过自动化流水线识别几何特征并分配有限元分析（FEA）标签。

Result: 仅使用不到 400 个初始设计，成功生成了 15,360 个带有仿真标签的 3D 托架数据集（扩大了 40 倍），在制造可行性、标签保真度和分布一致性方面均表现出高质量。

Conclusion: DeepJEB++ 证明了通过在 2D 潜在空间进行增强并结合领域自适应生成模型，可以高效地从有限的初始设计中构建大规模、具有物理标签的 3D 工程数据集，从而弥补了工程设计领域缺乏大规模 3D 数据集的瓶颈。

Abstract: Data-driven engineering design is constrained by the lack of large-scale 3D datasets that pair geometry with physics-based performance labels. In particular, existing 3D data augmentation techniques have limitations in preserving subtle and diverse geometric variations, and it remains difficult to automate the subsequent simulation-labeling process, where boundary conditions vary depending on the generated geometry. We present DeepJEB++, a foundation-model-driven data-augmentation framework that expands a small seed set of jet engine brackets into a large, simulation-labeled 3D dataset under constrained resources. Our key idea is to augment in the data-rich 2D latent space, then transfer to 3D. In Stage 1, we fine-tune a pretrained 2D latent diffusion model on multi-view renders and synthesize novel views by latent interpolation, retaining manufacturable designs through a vision-language-model (VLM) quality filter. In Stage 2, the validated images are lifted to 3D meshes by a domain-adapted generative foundation model. In Stage 3, an automated pipeline recognizes the load and bolt interfaces on each mesh and assigns finite-element labels -- mass, stress, and displacement -- without manual intervention. We assess augmentation quality along three intrinsic axes: manufacturability, label fidelity against the SimJEB ground truth, and distributional consistency. Starting from fewer than 400 seed designs, DeepJEB++ yields 15,360 simulation-labeled 3D brackets -- a 40x expansion -- using a single GPU per stage. The dataset will be made publicly available to support reproducible engineering-AI research.

### [133] [Reliability of Probabilistic Emulation of Physical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.12997)
*Sam F. Greenbury,Radka Jersakova,Paolo Conti,Marjan Famili,Christopher Iliffe Sprague,Edwin Brown,Jason D. McEwen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了物理系统概率预测的两大主流范式，发现使用CRPS训练的确定性集合模型在不确定性估计的可靠性及推理效率上，普遍优于目前主流的潜空间生成模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前物理系统概率预测主要有两种主流方法：基于生成模型的方法和CRPS训练的集合模型。尽管两者都表现出良好的预测精度，但学术界目前缺乏关于这两种方法在不确定性量化可靠性上的系统性对比分析，因此作者旨在弥补这一研究空白。

Method: 开发了一个统一的评估框架，在多种2D时空物理系统中，对生成模型（扩散模型/流匹配）与采用CRPS损失函数训练的确定性模型集合进行了对比。评估指标包括预测区间的经验覆盖率、预测精度以及推理效率。同时，研究者发布了AutoCast框架和AutoSim数据集生成工具以支持复现和扩展研究。

Result: 1. CRPS训练的集合模型在单步预测和自回归推演中均表现出更可靠的预测区间覆盖率；2. 与之相比，潜空间生成模型在不确定性可靠性上较差；3. 全空间训练的生成模型虽然在覆盖率上与CRPS集合相当，但推理延迟显著更高；4. CRPS集合模型在潜空间和全空间训练时表现一致，稳定性更强。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在保持计算预算和模型规模一致的条件下，CRPS训练的集合模型在预测不确定性的可靠性方面优于在潜空间中训练的生成模型，且推理速度更快。直接在全空间（ambient space）中训练生成模型可以达到类似CRPS集合的可靠性，但推理成本极其高昂。该研究通过AutoCast框架证实了CRPS方法在实际应用中的高效与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Two dominant approaches have emerged for generating probabilistic forecasts of physical systems: generative models, such as diffusion or flow matching; and ensembles of deterministic models with stochasticity injected, trained using the continuous ranked probability score (CRPS) loss. While both approaches have demonstrated strong predictive accuracy, the reliability of their uncertainties has not been systematically assessed. We address this gap by developing a framework to evaluate both approaches across diverse 2D spatiotemporal physical systems, under matched model size and computational budget. We assess the reliability of probabilistic emulation by inspecting the empirical coverage of predictive intervals, while also considering accuracy and computational efficiency metrics. CRPS-trained ensembles typically achieve more reliable uncertainties on both single-step prediction and autoregressive rollouts, demonstrating better coverage than the standard alternative of training generative models in a latent space. Moreover, the CRPS approach offers significantly faster inference. When generative models are trained in ambient rather than a compressed latent space, which is often infeasible for high-dimensional problems, they exhibit comparable coverage to CRPS-trained ensembles, though with substantially larger inference latency. In contrast, when CRPS-trained ensembles are trained in latent space they do not show a marked degradation in coverage with respect to ambient space. Both generative models and CRPS-trained ensembles demonstrate good predictive accuracy. To facilitate future research and application, we release AutoCast, a modular framework implementing both generative models and CRPS-trained ensembles, alongside AutoSim, a flexible dataset generation package for rapid prototyping.

However, existing methods focus on mining numerical statistical patterns, suffering from semantic agnosticism by neglecting the intrinsic biological functions encoded by genes. While Large Language Models (LLMs) offer promising semantic capabilities, their direct adaptation to cell clustering is hindered by the structural mismatch between generative pre-training objectives and discriminative downstream tasks. To bridge this gap, we propose scLLM-DSC, a novel LLM-Knowledge Enhanced Cross-Modal Deep Structural Clustering framework. Diverging from data-driven paradigms, scLLM-DSC establishes a semantically-grounded representation by synergizing two views: a Knowledge-Driven Semantic View derived from NCBI gene priors and contextualized Cell2Sentence embeddings, and a Structure-Aware Topological View extracted via a graph-guided encoder. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Granger Causal Discovery (GCD) is fundamental for analyzing temporal dependencies in complex systems. However, existing neural GCD methods predominantly rely on a "one-size-fits-all" paradigm, struggling to capture distribution shifts and dynamic regime changes inherent in real-world time series. This often leads to entangled representations and spurious causal graphs. In this paper, we propose CausalMoE, a billion-scale multimodal Granger causal foundation model that explicitly models patch-level heterogeneity. CausalMoE introduces a Pattern-Routed Mixture of Heterogeneous Experts, which dynamically identifies latent temporal patterns and routes patches to specialized domain experts, effectively decoupling regime-specific mechanisms from shared dynamics. To ensure interpretable graph recovery, we design a Causality-Aware Self-Attention mechanism operating across variables, yielding sparse Granger causal graphs via proximal optimization. Furthermore, CausalMoE is the first to integrate LLMs and VLMs to align numerical signals with textual and visual priors, regularizing causal estimation in complex scenarios. ### [136] [TWLA: Achieving Ternary Weights and Low-Bit Activations for LLMs via Post-Training Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13054)
*Zhixiong Zhao,Zukang Xu,Zhixuan Chen,Xing Hu,Zhe Jiang,Dawei Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 TWLA 的大模型后训练量化框架，通过权重三元化重塑和层间感知激活混合精度策略，在保持高精度的同时，实现了 1.58-bit 权重和 4-bit 激活的极低比特压缩，解决了大模型部署的内存与算力瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型（LLM）能力强大，但其巨大的内存和算力需求限制了部署。现有三元化方法难以处理激活值的长尾分布，导致激活值必须保持高精度，从而限制了端到端的推理加速。作者旨在通过高效的后训练量化（PTQ）技术，在保持高精度的前提下实现极低比特（1.58-bit 权重，4-bit 激活）的压缩。

Method: TWLA 框架包含三个关键组件：(1) E2M-ATQ：通过两阶段优化（从欧几里得空间初始化到流形重定位）最小化权重三元化带来的层输出误差；(2) KOTMS：利用 Kronecker 结构正交旋转将权重塑形为三元友好的三峰分布，并抑制激活异常值；(3) ILA-AMP：考虑层间二阶交互成本，联合优化层级比特分配，以防止因层间差异导致的精度级联下降。

Result: 实验结果表明，TWLA 在 W1.58A4 量化配置下，不仅保持了与全精度模型相近的高准确率，而且显著降低了模型的内存占用和计算复杂度，实现了有效的端到端推理加速。

Conclusion: TWLA 通过一种创新的三阶段量化框架（E2M-ATQ、KOTMS 和 ILA-AMP），成功解决了大语言模型在三元权重和低位激活下的精度损失问题，证明了极低比特量化（W1.58A4）在保持模型高性能的同时实现显著推理加速的可行性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) exhibit exceptional general language processing capabilities, but their memory and compute costs hinder deployment. Ternarization has emerged as a promising compression technique, offering significant reductions in model size and inference complexity. However, existing methods struggle with heavy-tailed activation distributions and therefore keep activations in high precision, fundamentally limiting end-to-end inference acceleration. To overcome this limitation, we propose TWLA, a post-training quantization (PTQ) framework that achieves 1.58-bit weight compression and 4-bit activation quantization while maintaining high accuracy. TWLA comprises three components: (1) Euclidean-to-Manifold Asymmetric Ternary Quantizer (E2M-ATQ) minimizes layer-output error under weight ternarization via a two-stage optimization from Euclidean initialization to manifold relocation; (2) Kronecker Orthogonal Tri-Modal Shaping (KOTMS) applies a Kronecker-structured orthogonal rotation to reshape weights into ternary-friendly tri-modal distributions, while the shared rotation statistically suppresses activation outliers; and (3) Inter-Layer Aware Activation Mixed Precision (ILA-AMP) explicitly introduces adjacent-layer second-order interaction costs in bit allocation and jointly optimizes for the layer-wise disparity of activation quantization gains induced by the shared orthogonal transform, preventing cascades triggered by a few weak layers. Extensive experiments demonstrate that TWLA maintains high accuracy under W1.58A4, while delivering significant inference acceleration. The code is available at <https://github.com/Kishon-zzx/TWLA>.

</details>

In this work, we transfer a pre-trained foundational model on QM9 targets to our application with minimal data requirements. Additionally, the pipeline integrates uncertainty quantification, allowing the user to gauge the confidence of the predictions. As baseline, we succeed in predicting the Hansen solubility parameters and Dielectric Constant for which extensive databases exist. Importantly, we achieve high model performance on additional targets, such as Gutmann Donor and Acceptor numbers, where the available data is extremely limited. Overall, we augment data on solubility descriptors by orders of magnitude with high quality predictions. ### [138] [Limits of spectral learning under noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13067)
*Sabin Roman,Ljupco Todorovski,Saso Dzeroski,Marta Sales-Pardo,Roger Guimera*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了谱方法在处理含噪数据时，系数估计存在一个本质的噪声稳定性阈值，并提出了一个由单一噪声尺度决定的通用退化模型，为理解函数逼近的固有极限提供了理论支撑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管谱方法在科学推断中广泛用于从含噪数据中学习函数关系，但其系数在噪声干扰下的稳定性缺乏深入的理论理解。本文旨在揭示噪声如何影响谱系数，并探索函数结构恢复的固有极限。

Method: 该研究采用了基于稀疏谱表示的监督回归方法，在多种基（Fourier, Legendre, Bessel, Haar）和维度下进行分析。通过对经验特征几何进行白化处理，推导出了含噪与无噪系数向量之间重叠的闭式解，并量化了噪声引起的系数漂移。

Result: 研究发现，噪声会导致学习到的系数向量产生可预测的漂移，其幅度取决于有效活跃谱模式的数量。结果表明，存在一条受单一内在噪声尺度支配的通用退化曲线，且数值实验证实了该理论预测的准确性。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了谱学习方法在从含噪数据中恢复函数结构时存在本质的噪声阈值。通过推导出的通用退化曲线，可以量化系数估计不稳定性与噪声水平之间的关系，为理解科学推断中的函数逼近极限提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Learning functional relationships from noisy data is a central problem in scientific inference. Spectral methods approximate unknown functions by expanding them in a basis and estimating the corresponding coefficients from data, but the stability of these coefficients under noise remains poorly understood. Here we study supervised regression with additive label noise using sparse spectral representations across multiple bases and dimensions. We show that noise induces a predictable drift in the learned coefficient vector whose magnitude depends on the effective number of active spectral modes. After whitening the empirical feature geometry, we derive a closed-form expression for the overlap between noisy and noiseless coefficient vectors, revealing a universal degradation curve governed by a single intrinsic noise scale. Numerical experiments across Fourier, Legendre, Bessel, and Haar bases confirm the theoretical prediction. The results demonstrate that spectral learning exhibits a fundamental noise threshold beyond which coefficient estimates become unstable, placing intrinsic limits on recovering functional structure from noisy data.

</details>

Results reveal improvements over the aforementioned backbones, providing evidence of Emotional Regulation as a promising method for defining emotion-augmented deep learning through artificial subjective experience. The study also enforces evidence of the impact of affective states in improving machine learning tasks' optimization, encouraging further investigation on emotion-inspired architectures.

### [140] [Scale Buys Interpolation, Structure Buys a Horizon: Certified Predictability for Equivariant World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13092)
*Hongbo Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了利用群等变性为世界模型提供“可预测时域”的数学证明。研究表明，单纯增加模型规模（Scale）无法保证预测可靠性，必须引入结构化约束（等变性）才能通过李雅普诺夫谱分析，实现对模型预测时域的量化审计与可靠性监控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型虽然规模巨大，但其平均预测误差无法反映特定预测的可靠性及预测时域的长短。作者旨在解决“如何衡量模型预测的可靠时域”这一问题，并证明单纯依靠模型规模化无法解决该问题，必须引入结构性约束（等变性）。

Method: 1. 理论推导：利用群等变性（Equivariance）推导出多步预测误差的证明，证明误差在对称轨道上保持恒定。
2. 李雅普诺夫谱分析：基于预测器的李雅普诺夫指数，分层计算预测时域 $T_j(\epsilon)$，提供预测误差的上限证明。
3. 实验验证：在 Lorenz-96 系统上对比等变网络与传统密集/循环网络。
4. 审计方法：提出无需校准数据的“训练前审计”方法，通过测量李雅普诺夫谱对现有预训练模型（如 TD-MPC2, V-JEPA）进行可靠性审计。

Result: 1. 理论上证明了只有等变模型才具有轨道恒定的误差属性。
2. 实验表明，在 Lorenz-96 系统中，仅 $\mathbb{Z}_N$ 等变网络能精准恢复完整的李雅普诺夫谱（$R^2=0.98$），而常规基准模型失败。
3. 验证了该方法可作为即插即用的监控工具，无需校准数据即可对大型预训练模型（如 1B 参数的 V-JEPA）进行可靠性审计，并能识别模型在不同状态下的预测表现（校准、乐观或保守）。

Conclusion: 该研究指出，单纯的规模化（Scale）仅能提升模型的插值能力，而无法保证预测的长期可靠性。只有通过引入群等变性（Equivariance）等结构化约束，才能获得可计算的、可靠的预测时域证明。这种基于李雅普诺夫谱的结构化认证机制，是评估和监控世界模型可靠性的必要手段。

Abstract: Scale buys interpolation; structure buys a certified horizon. A world model's average error says nothing about whether a particular prediction can be trusted, or for how long. For equivariant latent world models we give a computable, multi-step certificate of the predictable horizon: $T$-step rollout error is provably constant over each symmetry orbit (Theorem A) and stratified channel-by-channel by the predictor's Lyapunov spectrum, $T_j(ε)\sim\log(1/ε)/λ_j$. The horizon is two-sided -- a matching lower bound makes approximate equivariance provably horizon-limited -- and the certificate is exclusive to structure: orbit-constant error characterizes equivariance, so no non-equivariant model has it at any scale. Empirically, on 40-D Lorenz-96 only a $\mathbb{Z}_N$-equivariant network recovers the full Lyapunov spectrum ($R^2{=}0.98$); dense and recurrent baselines fail.
  Because the spectrum is faithful, the certificate acts, a priori: under a fixed sensing budget a $c\times$-inflated certificate provably needs $c\times$ the budget, and the equivariant certificate meets a budget its inflated dense counterpart cannot -- with zero calibration data. The same read-out, unchanged, audits public pretrained world models training-free: TD-MPC2 checkpoints land on the certificate's own scope taxonomy -- calibrated where strongly expansive (ratio 0.94-1.02), optimistic where weakly expansive, correctly abstaining where contracting -- a map a deployed monitor replicates cell-by-cell, out-of-sample. Across the official 1M-317M multitask ladder, calibration does not improve with parameters. On V-JEPA 2-AC (1B, real robot data) the measured cross-check correctly overrides an over-promising tangent spectrum -- the cross-validated audit, not the raw number, is the deployable object. Scale buys interpolation, not a calibrated horizon.

</details>


### [141] [Authority, Truth, and Citation Bias: A Large-Scale Multi-Domain Benchmark for Studying Epistemic Susceptibility in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13104)
*Aryan Khurana,Aravind Ramana RN,Dhruv Kumar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文推出了AuthorityBench基准测试，揭示了大型语言模型容易被“引用”这一权威信号误导，导致即便事实正确也会因虚假引用而产生严重幻觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究大语言模型在引用增强设置下，引用本身这一“权威信号”如何独立于事实内容之外影响模型的认知行为，以及这种信号是否会导致模型产生幻觉。

Method: 构建了名为 AuthorityBench 的大规模基准测试（包含220,564个提示词），采用2x2因子设计（交叉验证事实真实性与引用真实性），涵盖四个领域、40种模板、不同级别的出版场所及作者背景。在七个大模型上评估了引用存在对模型认知行为的影响。

Result: 引用（无论真实与否）均会显著增加模型的幻觉率；当虚假引用出现在正确声明中时，幻觉率上升最严重（增加3-22个百分点，在常识领域甚至高达35-77%）；法律领域相对稳健；出版场所声望与作者人口学特征对结果影响较小。

Conclusion: 引用作为权威信号会诱导大语言模型产生过度信任，导致模型即便面对已知事实也更倾向于生成虚假内容。研究表明，单纯依赖引用进行事实核查是不可靠的，未来的模型开发需降低对引用外观的认知权重。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed in citation-augmented settings, yet the effect of citation presence on model behavior independent of factual content remains poorly understood. We introduce AuthorityBench, a 220,564-prompt multi-domain benchmark that isolates how citation-based authority signals influence epistemic behavior in LLMs. The benchmark uses a fully balanced 2x2 factorial design crossing claim veracity with citation veracity, the first to do so, across four domains (general knowledge, science, law, and medicine), with controlled variation over 40 prompt templates, four venue prestige tiers, and a country-coded author name dataset. Evaluating seven models on 12 structured research questions, we find that citation presence, whether real or fabricated, consistently increases hallucination rates relative to a no-citation baseline. The effect is strongest when fabricated citations accompany true claims, raising hallucination rates by 3 to 22 percentage points and reaching 35 to 77% in the general knowledge domain, while legal claims are comparatively robust and venue prestige and author demographics show negligible impact. All datasets and evaluation code are available at: https://github.com/floating-reeds/AuthorityBench

### [142] [Disparate Impact in Synthetic Data Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13105)
*Paul Andrey,Michaël Perrot,Batiste Le Bars,Marc Tommasi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了合成数据生成中的“差异化影响”问题，指出其根本原因是模型拟合能力在不同群体间的偏差。研究提出通过分组学习策略，减少采样和隐私保护带来的误差，从而在提升数据效用的同时实现更公平的数据生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的公平合成数据生成（SDG）研究往往错误地试图修正观测数据中的偏差，导致生成的数据分布偏离了原始数据。本文旨在纠正这一认知，指出差异化影响的根源在于模型在不同群体上的拟合误差不一致，并寻求在保持真实分布还原性的同时实现公平性。

Method: 1. 重新定义合成数据生成（SDG）中的差异化影响，将其视作模型无法完美拟合真实数据分布的结果。2. 分析了SDG方法在面对不同群体时产生近似误差和估计误差的根源（包括表达能力限制、采样偏差、差分隐私机制带来的扰动）。3. 提出了一种“分组学习”（group-wise）的SDG模型训练策略，即针对不同敏感群体分别建模以减少偏差。

Result: 通过实验分析，揭示了概率图模型在处理小群体或高复杂度分布时，受采样噪声和差分隐私影响而产生的表现差异。结果证实，所提出的分组学习策略不仅能够提升整体的数据效用，还能显著缩小不同群体间在模型效用上的差距，从而实现更好的公平性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过针对不同群体分别训练生成模型（Group-wise SDG），可以有效缓解合成数据生成中的差异化影响问题，从而在保持整体效用的同时提升公平性。作者强调，确保合成数据与真实数据分布一致是实现公平性的根本，而非通过有偏的数据分布来定义所谓的公平。

Abstract: We revisit the fairness notion of disparate impact for synthetic data generation (SDG), that assesses whether the utility of generated records is the same across sensitive groups. Our approach departs from existing work on fair SDG, that address the problem of correcting for undue biases in the observed distribution, hence redefining SDG as learning a distribution that is not that of the real data. By contrast, non-disparate impact is notably achieved when the synthetic and real distributions are the same. We expose reasons why SDG may fail to reach that solution and discuss why approximation and estimation errors occur and can be disparate across groups. We notably look into the expressive power of SDG methods relative to distribution complexity, sampling errors due to group proportions, and estimation errors induced by differential privacy mechanisms. We illustrate cases of disparate impact on both artificial and real-world data, focusing on SDG methods that rely on probabilistic graphical models. We also introduce a strategy of learning group-wise SDG models and illustrate how it can improve both the overall utility and its parity in many settings.

### [143] [Demystifying Hidden-State Recurrence: Switchable Latent Reasoning with On-Policy Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13106)
*Jiayu Yang,Chao Chen,Shengen Wu,Yinhong Liu,Yuxuan Fan,Lujundong Li,Songning Lai,Chengwei Qin,Zhijiang Guo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出SWITCH框架，通过在隐空间推理中加入显式边界标记，解决了隐空间模型难以进行强化学习优化及缺乏可解释性的痛点，实现了性能提升与内部机制分析的统一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的隐空间推理方法难以利用标准在线强化学习（on-policy RL）进行优化，且其因果机制不透明，缺乏可解释性，限制了模型性能与安全性。

Method: 提出了SWITCH框架，通过定义`<swi>`和`</swi>`作为显式边界标记，使隐状态循环过程能够通过标准的强化学习算法（如GRPO）进行优化，并配合可见到隐式的训练课程（curriculum learning）以及反向传播梯度优化。

Result: SWITCH框架在同等规模下性能优于以往的隐状态循环推理方法。分析发现：`<swi>`是学习到的策略而非风格化伪影；隐空间计算具有针对性的因果重要性；且该计算过程高度集中于进入时的单次状态转换。

Conclusion: 研究证明，通过引入显式边界标记，隐空间推理（Latent CoT）不仅可以实现与标准强化学习算法的兼容，还能通过机械可解释性方法深入剖析其内部计算过程，为提升模型推理能力和透明度提供了新途径。

Abstract: Latent chain-of-thought compresses reasoning by replacing visible reasoning traces with continuous hidden-state recurrence, but existing formulations are difficult to optimize with standard on-policy reinforcement learning (RL) and hard to interpret causally. Our key insight is that a single pair of explicit boundary tokens can address both issues at once: discrete entry and exit anchors make the latent block compatible with standard on-policy RL, and the same anchors offer a natural foothold for mechanistic analysis. Motivated by this, we propose SWITCH, a switchable latent reasoning framework. The model emits <swi> to enter latent mode and </swi> to exit. Because the boundaries are ordinary discrete tokens, the GRPO policy ratio is well-defined at every decision point. The same anchors also expose the latent steps to direct probing and causal intervention. We train the model with a visible-to-latent curriculum and a Switch-GRPO objective that propagates gradients through recurrent latent computation. SWITCH consistently outperforms prior hidden-state-recurrence latent reasoning approaches at similar scale. Mechanistic analysis through the boundary tokens further reveals three findings: (i) <swi> is a sharply localised, learned switching policy rather than a stylistic artefact; (ii) the latent step it opens performs problem-specific, causally important computation rather than acting as an inert placeholder; and (iii) that computation is concentrated at a single hidden-state transition on entry. Together, these results show that hidden-state-recurrence latent reasoning is both RL-trainable and open to direct mechanistic analysis, including of how on-policy RL itself improves the model from the inside.

</details>


### [144] [MP3: Multi-Period Pattern Pre-training forSpatio-Temporal Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13119)
*Lilan Peng,Yandi Liu,Qingren Yao,Chongshou Li,Tianrui Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 MP3 的即插即用预训练插件，专门用于解决时空预测中的“时间海市蜃楼”难题。通过学习长时序中的多周期模式并捕捉跨周期因果关系，MP3 能显著提升各类现有 STGNN 模型的预测精度与鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的时空图神经网络（STGNN）在处理“时间海市蜃楼”（Temporal Mirage，即相似的短窗口输入对应不同的未来趋势，反之亦然）现象时效果不佳。作者认为其根本原因在于短窗口输入缺乏完整周期观测、空间相关性异构以及存在跨周期叠加因果关系，因此提出 MP3 以弥补这些缺陷。

Method: MP3 框架包含两大核心创新：1. 多周期模式学习：利用边缘卷积识别不同周期模式，通过瓶颈投影和全局记忆库捕捉异构全局空间关系。2. 跨周期模式交互：采用因果增强型 Transformer 来捕获不同周期模式之间的因果依赖关系。该框架设计为即插即用的插件，可无缝集成到现有的 STGNN 主干网络中。

Result: 在五个真实世界数据集上对五个 STGNN 基线模型进行的实验表明，MP3 具有优越的可扩展性和适应性，能够持续提升所有基线模型的性能。实验结果显示，引入 MP3 后，平均 MAE 降低了 4.7%，RMSE 降低了 5.0%。

Conclusion: MP3 框架通过引入多周期模式学习和跨周期模式交互，成功解决了现有 STGNN 模型难以处理“时间海市蜃楼”现象的问题。该插件具备极高的通用性和可扩展性，能够作为即插即用的模块显著提升各类现有时空预测模型的性能，为解决复杂时空数据中的长周期关联和异构空间依赖提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Spatio-Temporal forecasting is crucial in diverse fields, such as transportation, climate, and energy. Urban spatio-temporal data exhibits temporal mirage: similar short-window inputs have divergent future trends, and vice versa. Existing spatio-temporal graph neural networks (STGNNs) cannot effectively identify such mirages. We argue that the core reason lies in the short-window inputs that have incomplete period observation, heterogeneous global spatial correlation, and cross-period superposition causality. To bridge this gap, we develop a novel Multi- Period Pattern Pre-training (MP3), a plug-and-play pre-training plugin for distinguishing temporal mirages. MP3 presents two core innovations: (1) The multi-period pattern learning is designed to learn multi-period patterns from long time series. Specifically, multi-period temporal modeling leverages edge convolution to identify different multi-period patterns. Multi-period spatial modeling uses a bottleneck project and a global memory bank to capture heterogeneous global spatial relations efficiently. Cross-period pattern interaction employs a causality-enhanced Transformer to capture dependencies across different period patterns. (2) This plugin can seamlessly integrate into existing STGNN backbones to strengthen their forecasting performance. The experiment on five STGNN baselines across five real-world datasets (including a large-scale dataset CA) verify the effectiveness, superior scalability and strong adaptability of MP3, which brings consistent and robust performance improvements across all evaluated baselines. On average, MP3 reduces the MAE 4.7% and the RMSE 5.0%. The code can be available at https://github.com/YAN-outlook/MP3.

</details>


### [145] [Select and Improve: Understanding the Mechanics of Post-Training for Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13125)
*Akshay Krishnamurthy,Audrey Huang,Nived Rajaraman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了强化学习提升模型推理能力的两个机理：多样化SFT数据支持“策略选择”，递进难度RL数据驱动“策略优化”，为提升推理模型性能提供了明确的指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管强化学习在推理和代码模型训练中应用广泛，但目前对其如何从机理层面提升模型能力的认知尚不清晰，缺乏系统性的解释。

Method: 研究团队以Qwen-2.5-1.5B模型为基础，设计了受控的数学推理实验，通过分析模型在不同SFT数据（策略多样性）和RL数据（难度演进）驱动下的内部变化，揭示了强化学习后训练过程中的学习动态。

Result: 研究发现RL训练并不单纯是“增强”已有能力，而是主要通过以下两点实现：一是“策略选择”，即通过SFT阶段引入多样化推理路径，使模型学会根据问题选择最优解法；二是“策略优化”，即通过RL训练中增加问题难度，迫使模型对现有策略进行改进和精炼。

Conclusion: 强化学习（RL）通过策略选择和策略优化两种核心机制提升模型推理能力。SFT阶段的数据多样性为模型提供了多种路径选择，而RL阶段的任务难度递进则推动了模型对这些路径的优化。这些发现为通过针对性的数据策略扩展推理能力提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning has rapidly emerged as a key component in the training of reasoning and coding models, yet it remains poorly understood from a mechanistic perspective. We study how and through what underlying processes capabilities are acquired or enhanced via reinforcement learning post-training. Our analysis, based on controlled math reasoning experiments with Qwen-2.5-1.5B, reveals two core mechanisms: strategy selection and strategy improvement. Our results highlight the role of SFT data and reinforcement learning data in activating these mechanisms, in particular showing how supervising the model on diverse reasoning strategies can enable strategy selection and how increasing difficulty in reinforcement learning data can enable strategy improvement. Taken together, our results provide mechanistic insight into RL training and suggest practical interventions to continue scaling reasoning capabilities.

### [146] [MiniPIC: Flexible Position-Independent Caching in <100LOC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13126)
*Nathan Ordonez,Thomas Parnell*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MiniPIC 是一种在 vLLM 中实现位置无关缓存（PIC）的轻量化方案。通过去除 KV 缓存中的位置旋转信息并引入细粒度的控制原语，MiniPIC 实现了高效的 KV 复用，显著降低了 RAG 和智能体任务的预填充延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在 RAG 和智能体任务中，系统频繁处理重复的结构化输入（如文档或代码片段）。现有的前缀缓存机制（如 vLLM 原生缓存）对输入对齐要求过严，而现有的位置无关缓存（PIC）实现方式通常需要大规模重构代码，或因跨设备数据传输导致性能损失。MiniPIC 旨在解决这些局限性，实现一种最小化、灵活且高效的缓存重用方案。

Method: MiniPIC 主要包含两项核心技术：1. 使用位置无关的 KV 缓存（即存储未旋转的 K 向量，在 Attention 计算时根据请求逻辑位置动态应用 RoPE）；2. 引入三个用户级控制原语（块对齐填充、跨度分隔符和提示依赖），用于精确管理缓存哈希行为和因果注意力结构。该方案通过不到 100 行的核心引擎改动和自定义注意力后端实现，并与现有的 CPU 卸载机制兼容。

Result: 在 2WikiMultihopQA 数据集上，MiniPIC 配合交错调度技术，将预填充吞吐量提升了 49%；缓存跨度的首字生成时间（TTFT）缩短了两个数量级；有效保持了非缓存跨度的线性扩展性，且在最坏情况下仅带来 5.7% 的额外开销。

Conclusion: MiniPIC 提供了一种轻量级、灵活且高效的缓存方案，证明了通过位置编码解耦和细粒度的控制原语，可以在主流推理引擎中以极小的代码改动实现位置无关的缓存（PIC），显著提升检索增强生成（RAG）和智能体任务的推理性能。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented and agentic workloads repeatedly prefill recurring predictable structured inputs (which we call "spans") such as documents and code files. Yet, prefix caching in engines such as vLLM cannot reuse their KV entries unless they share identical prefixes with another request, while Position-Independent Caching (PIC) implementations within production-grade inference servers typically either require substantial server code changes or keep KV state outside the server, incurring host-to-device transfer overhead. We present Minimalistic PIC (MiniPIC): a minimal, flexible and fast vLLM design built from two ingredients: positional-encoding-free KV cache and user-controlled cache-reuse primitives. MiniPIC stores unrotated K vectors in the KV cache, applies RoPE to K tiles inside attention using per-request logical positions, and exposes three user-facing and token-level primitives: block-aligned padding, span separator (SSep), and prompt depend (PDep), that modify hashing behavior and effective block-level causal attention structure. With fewer than 100 lines of core-engine changes plus a custom attention backend, these primitives are sufficient to realize multiple PIC methods, including Block-Attention, EPIC, and Prompt Cache, within the same running vLLM instance, while natively integrating with KV cache CPU offload implementations. On 2WikiMultihopQA, MiniPIC with interleaved scheduling improves prefill throughput by 49% over baseline vLLM, reduces cached-span time-to-first-token by up to two orders of magnitude, preserves the linear prefill scaling of uncached spans, and incurs only 5.7% worst-case overhead.

</details>


### [147] [When Does Routing Become Interpretable? Causal Probes on Block Attention Residuals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13168)
*Aydin Javadov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了Block AttnRes架构通过暴露路由权重进行可解释性分析的潜力，结论指出路由的直观显示并不足以直接等同于模型机制，必须通过因果干预进行验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Block AttnRes通过将固定的加性残差替换为跨层路由的softmax权重，使得深度路由成为可观测的张量，理论上为机制可解释性提供了新的视角。作者旨在探究这种架构上的可观测性是否足以直接推断模型内部的计算机制，还是需要进一步的验证。

Method: 研究通过对比两个同等规模（0.6B）的Qwen3模型进行探究：一是通过确定性最近偏差（recency-bias）调度的基准模型（路由权重与内容无关），二是将路由作为优化一部分进行从头训练的Block AttnRes模型。研究采用了路由消融干预（routing-ablation interventions）来对比分析路由权重（Mass）与因果重要性（Causal Importance）之间的关系。

Result: 实验发现：1. 训练后的AttnRes模型表现出局部化的路由模式（如嵌入源路径、当前状态路径和旧历史路径）；2. 路由权重（Mass）与因果重要性之间存在显著脱节，即路由权重占比最高的部分并不一定具有最高的因果贡献，且部分具备权重的路径在干预下并无明显的因果角色。

Conclusion: 仅仅通过架构设计暴露路由信息不足以进行机制可解释性分析。尽管深度路由在训练过程中能形成结构化模式，但描述性的路由权重并不直接等同于因果机制。研究强调，可解释性研究必须将路由分析视为待验证的假设，必须结合因果干预手段才能确定其真实的机制作用。

Abstract: Block Attention Residuals (Block AttnRes) by replace fixed additive residuals with a learned softmax over earlier depth-source representations, surfacing cross-layer routing as an inspectable tensor in the forward pass. This is a tempting interpretability target: information flow normally inferred indirectly is now directly observable. We ask whether such exposure suffices for mechanistic interpretation. We probe two same-scale ($0.6$B) Block AttnRes checkpoints under identical routing-ablation interventions: a vanilla Qwen3 inference-wrapped through a deterministic recency-bias schedule that the codebase admits as a routing-equivalent loading path, and a Block AttnRes Qwen3 trained from scratch with routing as part of optimisation. The wrapped baseline's routing weights are content-independent and reproduce the schedule's analytic prediction. The trained AttnRes checkpoint instead exhibits three localised routing motifs: an embedding-source pathway through early-layer MLP, a current-state pathway through early-layer attention and MLP, and an older-history pathway through late-layer attention. Beyond this stratification, we find a sharp dissociation between average routing mass and causal importance: in both sublayers, the largest mass slice is not the largest causal contribution, and one source family carries appreciable mass with no detectable causal role under intervention. Architectural exposure of routing is therefore necessary but not sufficient for mechanistic interpretation: structured depth routing emerges only when routing has been part of training, and even then, descriptive routing summaries should be treated as candidate hypotheses to be tested by causal interventions, not as evidence of mechanism in their own right.

</details>


### [148] [Detecting Explanatory Insufficiency in Learned Representations: A Framework for Representational Vigilance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13172)
*Jacques Raynal,Pierre Slangen,Elsa Raynal,Jacques Margerit*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了VER框架，用于诊断机器学习模型中被传统指标忽略的、持久的表征残差结构，旨在通过系统的监测流程提升模型表征的充分性与解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器学习评估主要侧重于预测性能、鲁棒性或泛化能力，但这些指标往往难以揭示模型表征中存在的、尚未被完全捕捉的持久性残差结构。研究者希望通过一个明确的诊断框架，识别模型表征中的“解释性不足”，以提升模型在复杂场景下的表征质量。

Method: 该研究引入了VER（Vigilant Evaluator of Representations）概念框架，这并非一种算法或模型架构，而是一套系统的诊断流程。该流程包括：表征识别、解释域界定、残差结构检测、解释阻力评估以及警示信号输出，旨在将解释性不足的潜在指标从噪声和普通预测误差中剥离出来。

Result: VER框架为评估表征充分性提供了一套标准化的监控序列。研究论证了该框架能够有效区分表征不足与常规的预测误差或数据噪声，并指明了通过构建“表征警示基准”（representational-vigilance benchmarks）来实现实证评估的路径。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的VER框架通过将表征充分性视为明确的研究对象，为机器学习模型诊断提供了一个互补性的评估维度。它强调在传统指标之外，应关注模型是否未能捕捉到持久的残差结构，从而弥补了现有评估方法在解释性不足方面的盲点。

Abstract: Learned representations are central to modern machine learning and are commonly evaluated through predictive performance, robustness, uncertainty estimation, or generalization. However, a learned representation may remain operationally successful while progressively failing to organize persistent residual structures that are not fully captured by conventional evaluation metrics. This article introduces VER, the Vigilant Evaluator of Representations, a conceptual framework for monitoring representational adequacy in learned representations. VER does not propose a new learning algorithm, loss function, or model architecture. Instead, it formalizes a diagnostic process through which persistent residual structures may be identified, analyzed, and interpreted as potential indicators of explanatory insufficiency. The framework distinguishes representational inadequacy from ordinary prediction error, uncertainty, noise, and distribution shift. It introduces a monitoring sequence based on representation identification, explanatory-domain delimitation, residual-structure detection, explanatory-resistance evaluation, and vigilance signaling. VER is intended as a contribution to representation diagnostics in machine learning. Its objective is not to replace existing evaluation methods but to complement them by treating representational adequacy as an explicit object of inquiry. A path toward empirical evaluation through representational-vigilance benchmarks is also outlined.

### [149] [Getting Better at Working With You: Compiling User Corrections into Runtime Enforcement for Coding Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13174)
*Yujun Zhou,Kehan Guo,Haomin Zhuang,Xiangqi Wang,Yue Huang,Zhenwen Liang,Pin-Yu Chen,Tian Gao,Nuno Moniz,Nitesh V. Chawla,Xiangliang Zhang*

TL;DR: 针对大模型智能体无法持久记忆用户偏好的痛点，本文提出了TRACE框架，通过将用户纠正转化为强制执行的运行时规则，实现了对智能体行为的有效约束，显著提升了偏好遵循的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的交互式大模型智能体存在“记忆与合规脱节”的问题，即用户在一次对话中提供的纠正意见，在后续会话中往往被智能体忽略，导致用户需要反复纠正，缺乏持久且可靠的偏好学习能力。

Method: 提出了TRACE（测试时规则获取与编译强制执行）框架。该方法通过挖掘用户的交互纠正意见，将其重写为原子规则，并在智能体执行任务前将这些规则编译为运行时检查程序，从而确保智能体行为符合用户偏好。

Conclusion: 研究表明，将用户的纠正反馈转化为可执行的原子规则并进行编译强制执行（TRACE），能够有效解决大模型智能体在跨会话中无法持续遵守用户偏好的问题，显著降低用户重复纠正的负担。

Abstract: Interactive LLM agents are becoming part of daily work, but they do not reliably become easier to work with over time: a correction remembered in one session may still be violated in the next. We study this gap between preference access and preference compliance. In tasks derived from anonymized real-user friction cases, Mem0 memory still leaves 57.5% of applicable preference checks violated. We introduce Test-time Rule Acquisition and Compiled Enforcement (TRACE), a drop-in skill-layer pipeline for coding-agent runtimes that mines user corrections, rewrites them as atomic rules, and compiles them into runtime checks that must pass before an agent completes future tasks. Unlike runtime checks written ahead of time by developers, TRACE skills come from the user's own chat corrections. We evaluate TRACE with simulated user-in-the-loop experiments on ClawArena coding-agent tasks and MemoryArena-derived memory-intensive tasks. On ClawArena, TRACE reduces held-out preference violation from 100.0% to 37.6% on in-distribution tasks and from 100.0% to 2.0% on out-of-distribution tasks. On MemoryArena-derived tasks, TRACE reduces in-distribution violation from 100.0% to 60.5% while matching or exceeding the strongest memory baseline on task pass. These results suggest that compiling corrections into runtime enforcement can address a repeated-friction failure mode that memory alone does not reliably solve, reducing the need for users to restate the same correction across future sessions. Experiment code is available at https://github.com/YujunZhou/TRACE_exp, and the deployable skill is available at https://github.com/YujunZhou/tellonce.

### [150] [Loss-Shift Transfer via Bayes Quotients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13178)
*Vasileios Sevetlidis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了迁移学习中一种被忽视的现象——“损失偏移”（loss shift），即在数据分布不变的情况下，因损失函数对信息需求精度的不同，会导致原有表征无法适配新任务，并从理论和实验上证明了这种信息丢弃带来的风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的迁移学习研究多关注分布偏移（distribution shift），但作者指出，即便在数据分布完全固定的情况下，若损失函数发生改变，也会产生一种正交的失败模式。该研究旨在解释为何相同的特征表示在不同的损失函数下表现迥异。

Method: 论文引入了“损失偏移”（loss shift）这一概念，并利用“贝叶斯商”（Bayes quotients）形式化定义了损失函数之间的精细化排序。作者推导了当损失函数发生变化时，过量风险（excess risk）与表征丢弃的信息之间的量化关系，并设计了涵盖合成数据、受控环境及真实图像的实验进行验证。

Result: 实验验证了预测结果：在固定数据分布的前提下，即使在分类任务中表现等价的表征，在面对不同的损失函数（尤其是对数损失）时，其性能也会出现显著差异。这也量化证明了损失函数精细度差异会导致表征信息的有效性损失。

Conclusion: 研究表明，即便在数据分布固定不变的情况下，不同的损失函数对表征学习的要求也不同。由于不同损失函数对信息的需求存在“精细度”差异，源任务的最小化表征往往不足以满足更精细的目标损失函数，这种表征的不适配性是导致迁移学习性能下降的关键因素之一。

Abstract: Transfer learning is usually studied as a consequence of distribution shift. This paper identifies an orthogonal failure mode in which the data distribution is fixed and the loss changes. This setting is called \emph{loss shift}. A loss determines which information in \(X\) is Bayes-relevant, and two losses may therefore require different representations even under the same joint law \(P(X,Y)\). The idea is formalized using Bayes quotients, which allow losses to be ordered by refinement. In the Bayes-quotient formulation, strict refinement gives an immediate qualitative obstruction. A source-minimal representation for a coarser loss is insufficient for a strictly finer target loss. For finite-output log loss, this obstruction becomes an exact quantitative identity. The excess risk is the conditional information about \(Y\) discarded by the representation. Experiments in controlled, learned, synthetic-image, and real-image settings show the predicted effect, i.e., classification-equivalent representations can have different optimal log-loss performance under a fixed data distribution.

</details>


### [151] [Understanding helpfulness and harmless tension in reward models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13209)
*Eshaan Tanwar,Pepa Atanasova*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文深入探讨了RLHF奖励模型中“帮助性”与“无害性”之间的冲突，通过神经元级的因果分析发现，由于大量神经元被两个目标共享且功能互斥，导致了对齐张力，这为理解多目标对齐的困难提供了机制性解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）中，奖励模型是核心组件，但人们对如何同时实现模型“有益”且“无害”的内部运作机制及其目标间的潜在冲突缺乏深入了解。研究旨在揭示这种对齐张力的机理。

Method: 研究采用了对比实验方法，分别训练了仅关注帮助性、仅关注无害性以及混合目标的奖励模型。同时，利用基于激活的分析技术识别与各目标相关的神经元，并通过针对性消融（Targeted Ablations）手段验证这些神经元对不同任务的因果影响，分析共享神经元的作用。

Result: 研究发现：1. 混合目标模型表现往往逊于单目标模型，证实了目标间存在干扰；2. 存在特定的神经元分别支持帮助性或无害性，且这些神经元对另一目标常有负面影响；3. 相当大比例的神经元在两个目标间共享，且这些共享神经元对模型行为影响巨大，是导致对齐张力的主要原因。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了奖励模型在对齐任务中存在“目标张力”（Alignment Tension），即帮助性（Helpfulness）与无害性（Harmlessness）在内部神经元层面上存在竞争与干扰。未来的对齐研究应转向更解耦、可控的模型架构，以缓解多目标对齐的内在冲突。

Abstract: Reward models are a key component of reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF), aligning language models toward both helpful and harmless behaviour. However, the internal mechanisms underlying these objectives and their conflicts remain poorly understood. We study alignment tension in reward models trained under helpfulness-only, harmlessness-only, and mixed-objective settings. We find that mixed-objective models often underperform single-objective models, indicating interference between objectives. Using activation-based methods, we identify neurons associated with each objective and study their functional roles via targeted ablations. We find that these neurons causally support their corresponding objectives while often negatively affecting the opposing one. We find that a substantial proportion of neurons are shared between helpfulness and harmlessness, and that these shared neurons exert a disproportionate influence on model behaviour, contributing to alignment tension. Additionally, our results provide insights and mechanistic interpretation into how alignment objectives are represented in reward models and why multi-objective alignment remains challenging, motivating future work on disentangled and controllable alignment methods.

### [152] [The Geometry of Phase Transitions in Generative Dynamics via Projection Caustics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13191)
*Ryosuke Sakamoto,Kotaro Sakamoto*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了扩散模型中生成突变的几何起源，指出其源于投影焦散现象。作者提出了临界边界检测器（CBD）来诊断这一不稳定性，并证明其在定位模式选择和支持生成过程精确控制方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型等连续状态生成模型虽然在理论上基于平滑的逆向时间动力学，但在实际生成过程中，样本轨迹往往表现出突发的质变（如模式坍缩、语义选择等）。现有研究缺乏对这种“相变”行为背后几何机制的深入解释，限制了对生成过程的精确控制。

Method: 1. 提出将去噪过程视为在自由能景观上的梯度下降；2. 论证了锐利转折（即模式选择）发生在投影焦散附近（即向数据支撑点的最近点投影不再唯一的位置）；3. 设计了临界边界检测器（CBD），用于检测分数方向的不稳定性，以此诊断模式承诺并识别干预敏感窗口。

Result: 1. 成功将扩散模型中观察到的突变现象与微分几何中的焦散理论联系起来；2. 验证了CBD在玩具模型、标准扩散模型及潜在文本到图像扩散模型中的有效性；3. 实验表明CBD能够精确定位模式承诺的时间点，预测对干预敏感的时间窗口，并支持在几何敏感区域进行定向控制。

Conclusion: 本研究通过引入临界边界检测器（CBD），揭示了扩散模型中样本生成过程的几何本质。研究表明，生成过程中的“相变”现象本质上是投影焦散（projection caustics）引起的，即当样本接近数据分布的奇异点时，投影不再唯一，从而导致生成轨迹发生突变。CBD提供了一种量化这种不稳定性的有效手段，为理解和控制生成过程提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Continuous-state generative samplers, including diffusion and flow-matching models, evolve through continuous reverse-time dynamics, yet their samples often undergo abrupt qualitative changes: trajectories commit to modes, semantic alternatives collapse, and small perturbations in narrow time windows can produce large downstream effects. This paper develops a geometric account of such phase-transition-like behaviour. We view denoising as gradient descent on a free energy landscape and show that sharp transitions arise near projection caustics, where the nearest-point projection onto the data support ceases to be unique. Motivated by this perspective, we introduce the Critical Boundary Detector (CBD), as practical diagnostics for score-direction instability. Across toy models, standard diffusion models, and latent text-to-image diffusion models, CBD localises mode commitment, predicts intervention-sensitive windows, and supports targeted control in geometrically sensitive regions. Our results connect geometry of data and dynamics of diffusion generation.

### [153] [WHAR Arena: Benchmarking the State of the Art in Efficient Wearable Human Activity Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13194)
*Maximilian Burzer,Tobias King,Till Riedel,Michael Beigl,Tobias Röddiger*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前WHAR领域存在严重的“可比性危机”，即由于数据集选择不一致、数据处理方式各异及评估协议不统一，导致目前所谓的“最先进水平（SOTA）”缺乏稳健性，难以进行公平比较。

Method: 建立了一个大规模开源基准测试框架，整合了30个不同的数据集，并采用标准化的数据处理流程和统一的跨受试者评估协议。研究评估了17种代表性架构，进行了4760次训练实验，并在Android设备上实测了预测性能、延迟、峰值内存占用和模型大小。

Result: 研究发现并没有单一的最优架构。虽然CNN-HAR在平均宏F1分数上略高，但各主流架构的预测性能已趋于瓶颈。在兼顾部署效率时，TinierHAR和随机森林等轻量级模型构成了更具实际价值的帕累托前沿，而大型递归或混合模型在未带来显著性能提升的同时，却消耗了极高的硬件资源。

Conclusion: 穿戴式人体活动识别（WHAR）领域的预测性能已趋于饱和。未来的研究重心应从单纯追求精度转向提升部署效率（轻量化）以及增强模型对领域偏移的适应能力。

Abstract: Deep learning has become the dominant paradigm in Wearable Human Activity Recognition (WHAR), yet progress is obscured by a comparability crisis. Results are often reported using inconsistent datasets, custom data processing, and varying evaluation protocols, making state-of-the-art claims fragile. We address this with a large-scale, open-source benchmark that integrates 30 diverse datasets under standardized processing, unified model interfaces, and a shared cross-subject evaluation protocol. Evaluating 17 representative architectures across 4760 training runs, we jointly measure predictive performance alongside on-device latency, peak memory, and model size on an Android reference device. Our results reveal that the WHAR state of the art is distributed rather than dominated by a single architecture. While CNN-HAR achieves the highest mean macro-F1, top-performing models cluster tightly, indicating contemporary architectures have converged near a predictive performance ceiling. When accounting for deployment efficiency, compact neural models, such as TinierHAR, and classical Random Forests define the practically relevant Pareto frontier, whereas larger recurrent and hybrid models incur high hardware costs without corresponding performance gains. Consequently, while predictive performance has plateaued, substantial potential for future progress remains in optimizing deployment efficiency and improving adaptation to domain shifts. We release our full framework to support transparent reuse and extension.

</details>


### [154] [MaxProof: Scaling Mathematical Proof with Generative-Verifier RL and Population-Level Test-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13473)
*Jiacheng Chen,Xinyu Zhang,Shunkai Zhang,Yanmohan Wang,Lin Li,Tiancheng Qin,Qin Wang,Zhengmao Zhu,Tianle Li,Jingyang Li,Zehan Li,Binyang Jiang,Jin Zhu,Han Ding,Fei Yu,Chenyu Du,Zijian Song,Jiayuan Song,Zhi Zhang,Yunan Huang,Weiyu Cheng,Pengyu Zhao,Yu Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了解决当前人工智能模型在处理竞赛级数学证明时推理能力不足的问题，作者旨在通过引入一种种群规模的测试时扩展框架，提高模型生成、验证及修复数学证明的精度与鲁棒性。

Method: 1. 训练阶段：构建 MiniMax-M3 系列模型，针对证明生成、证明验证和基于批判（critique）的证明修复三种能力进行训练，并使用低误报率的“深度防御”生成式验证器。2. 测试阶段（MaxProof）：将模型视作生成器、验证器、修正器和排序器的统一体，在证明候选集合上进行搜索，并通过锦标赛选择（tournament selection）机制筛选出最终的最优证明。

Result: 在应用 MaxProof 框架后，M3 模型在 IMO 2025 比赛中获得 35/42 分，在 USAMO 2026 比赛中获得 36/42 分，得分均超过了人类金牌的门槛。

Conclusion: MaxProof 框架通过结合种群规模的测试时扩展（test-time scaling）与多维度生成与验证策略，显著提升了模型在顶尖数学竞赛题目上的表现，证明了这种结合验证、修复和锦标赛选择的系统在处理复杂推理任务上的优越性，达到了超越人类金牌选手的水平。

Abstract: We present MaxProof, a population-level test-time scaling framework for competition-level mathematical proof in the MiniMax-M3 series. M3 first trains three proof-oriented capabilities -- proof generation, proof verification, and critique-conditioned proof repair -- using a defense-in-depth generative verifier engineered for low false-positive rate. These capabilities are merged into a single released M3 model. At test time, MaxProof treats the model as a generator, verifier, refiner, and ranker, searches over a population of candidate proofs, and returns one final proof through tournament selection. With MaxProof test-time scaling, the M3 model reaches 35/42 on IMO 2025 and 36/42 on USAMO 2026, exceeding the human gold-medal threshold on both.

Conclusion: 本文推出的SupraBench和SupraPMC为超分子化学领域的AI研究提供了关键基础。实验表明，现有的LLM在处理超分子化学推理任务时仍有较大改进空间。领域自适应预训练虽然能提升回归任务性能，但会对格式遵循能力产生负面影响，揭示了模型在跨领域推理与指令遵循之间的权衡。

Abstract: Supramolecular chemistry, which includes the study of non-covalent host-guest assemblies, has advanced various applications. Our source codes and benchmark datasets are available at https://github.com/Tianyi-Billy-Ma/SupraBench.

### [156] [From Uncertain Judgments to Calibrated Rankings: Conformal Elo Estimation for LLM Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13221)
*Bora Kargi,David Salinas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型自动评估中存在的系统性偏差，研究提出了一种结合“软标签”Bradley-Terry建模与一致性预测的框架，能够在无需大规模人工干预的情况下，生成校准后的模型排名及可靠的不确定性边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的“LLM作为裁判”（LLM-as-a-judge）评估方法存在位置偏差、自偏好和不可传递性等系统性误差，导致模型排名失准；而传统人工标注成本高昂，因此需要一种既低成本又能校准排名、量化不确定性的自动化评估工具。

Method: 1. 局部层面：不再使用硬标签，而是通过传播校准后的胜率（win probabilities）进入Bradley-Terry模型，计算评估过程中的不确定性。
2. 全局层面：应用分裂一致性预测（split conformal prediction）来处理LLM评分与人工评分之间的残差差距，从而为模型排名提供具备分布无关边际覆盖保证的预测区间。

Result: 该方法在LMArena数据集上表现出色，仅通过LLM评分即可将Elo估计与人工评分的平均绝对误差（MAE）降低至17.9以内，并能为模型排名提供稳健的预测区间，有效提升了自动评估的准确性和可信度。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种利用“软”判定（Soft-Judge）改进大语言模型自动评估的方法，通过在局部层面进行不确定性量化并在全局层面提供预测区间，无需大规模人工标注即可获得校准后的Elo评分和诚实的置信区间，为大模型的高效评估提供了可靠的框架。

Abstract: Evaluating new large language models typically requires costly human annotation campaigns at scale. LLM-as-a-judge offers a cheaper alternative, but judge scores carry systematic errors - such as position bias, self-preference, or intransitivity - that can strongly miscalibrate the resulting rankings. We quantify the resulting judge-human disagreement at two complementary levels. At the local level, we estimate per-battle uncertainty from the judge's own score differences by propagating calibrated win probabilities rather than hard labels into the Bradley-Terry procedure. This alone provides a drastic improvement to Elo estimation accuracy, bringing LLM-derived ratings within 17.9 Elo MAE of human-derived ones when averaged over 55 held-out models on LMArena. At the global level, we apply split conformal prediction to the residual gap between LLM-derived and human-derived Elo ratings across held-out models, producing prediction intervals with distribution-free marginal coverage guarantees that account for irreducible LLM-human disagreement. Together, these two layers yield a low-cost evaluation tool that provides developers with calibrated Elo estimates and honest uncertainty bounds, without access to large-scale human annotations.To facilitate reproducibility, we release our code at https://github.com/kargibora/SoftElo .

</details>

Method: 提出了一种新的监督分类损失函数概念，不再将输入样本强制映射到单一标签，而是定义了一个涵盖所有分类器输出的双峰高斯分布作为优化目标，以此建模类别模糊性。

Result: 实验表明该方法在提升模型鲁棒性方面具有显著效果，特别是在训练数据匮乏的情况下提升更为明显，且仅需对标准训练流程进行微小改动。

Abstract: This paper proposes a novel loss concept for supervised classification tasks. This softer target formulation implicitly captures class ambiguity, mitigates overfitting, and encourages the learning of more robust decision boundaries, all without requiring additional label information. Experimental results demonstrate consistent improvements in robustness, with particularly pronounced gains in low-data regimes, while requiring only minimal modifications to standard training pipelines.

### [158] [ReSET: Accurate Latency-Critical NVFP4 Reasoning via Step-Aware Temperature Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13233)
*Sihwa Lee,Janghwan Lee,Donghoon Yoo,Jae Gon Kim,Hanyul Ryu,Soojung Ryu,Jungwook Choi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大型推理模型在NVFP4量化下的精度退化和延迟问题，本文提出了ReSET自适应解码策略与新型NVFP4优化算子，在保持推理精度的同时显著提升了推理速度与计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理模型（LRM）虽然推理能力强但计算成本高；虽然NVFP4量化可降低成本，但直接应用会导致推理精度下降，且现有的NVFP4算子在小批次解码场景下无法有效提升延迟表现。

Method: 1. 分析NVFP4量化对推理过程中Token级不确定性的影响，发现其会导致符号Token采样错误及高不确定性步骤中的Token过度集中；2. 提出ReSET方法，通过基于推理步骤的熵自适应调整解码温度；3. 设计CUDA-core small-M NVFP4算子，专门优化延迟敏感的小批次自回归解码。

Result: ReSET方法使NVFP4的推理准确率提升了约2个百分点；优化的CUDA-core small-M算子实现了相比vLLM NVFP4最高2.5倍的核级加速，以及相比BF16约2倍的端到端解码速度提升。

Conclusion: 本研究通过提出的ReSET解码策略和优化的NVFP4算子，成功克服了大型推理模型在低精度量化下的精度损失与延迟瓶颈，证明了硬件支持的低精度推理在复杂推理任务中的可行性与高效性。

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) improve complex problem-solving by generating long intermediate reasoning traces, but this substantially increases inference costs. NVFP4 inference offers a promising approach to reduce both computational and memory costs through hardware-supported low-precision execution. However, directly applying NVFP4 to LRMs introduces two practical limitations: reasoning accuracy degrades under quantization, and existing NVFP4 kernels do not fully realize latency benefits in small-batch autoregressive decoding. In this work, we analyze the effect of NVFP4 quantization on token-level uncertainty during reasoning. We show that quantization increases incorrect sampling at low-entropy symbolic tokens, while causing over-concentration on a small set of tokens in high-uncertainty reasoning steps. Based on this observation, we propose \textbf{ReSET}, a reasoning-step entropy-based temperature-scaling method that estimates step-level uncertainty online and adapts the decoding temperature using both token-level and step-level entropy signals. To address the latency gap, we further design a CUDA-core small-$M$ NVFP4 kernel for latency-critical autoregressive decoding. Across reasoning benchmarks and model scales, ReSET improves NVFP4 reasoning accuracy by up to $\sim\!$2 points over the NVFP4 baseline. Our CUDA-core small-$M$ kernel further improves latency-critical decoding, delivering up to $2.5\!\times$ kernel-level speedup over NVFP4 vLLM and approximately $2\!\times$ end-to-end decoding speedup over BF16. Code is available at https://github.com/aiha-lab/ReSET.

</details>


### [159] [Beyond the Commitment Boundary: Probing Epiphenomenal Chain-of-Thought in Large Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13603)
*Daniel Scalena,Sara Candussio,Luca Bortolussi,Elisabetta Fersini,Malvina Nissim,Gabriele Sarti*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了思维链（CoT）推理中存在“承诺边界”现象，即模型往往在推理中途即已确定最终答案，后续步骤多为冗余。研究据此提出了一种基于提前退出的优化方法，在保持模型性能的同时，可将思维链长度平均缩短55%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的思维链（CoT）推理范式虽然流行，但学术界对于思维链中各个具体步骤对最终答案的因果影响机制缺乏深入理解，且现有的推理过程可能存在大量冗余计算。

Method: 1. 利用“提前退出（early exit）”技术评估思维链中各推理步骤的因果重要性；2. 定义并观察“承诺边界（commitment boundary）”，即模型从中间猜测向稳定高置信度答案转换的临界点；3. 使用注意力探测（attention probes）从中间步骤线性解码最终答案；4. 基于解码出的答案形成信号，提出一种动态提前退出机制。

Result: 1. 发现思维链中存在“承诺边界”，推理通常在极短步骤内完成从猜测到稳定答案的转变；2. 转换点后的步骤多为“附带现象（epiphenomenal）”，对最终结果无实质影响；3. 答案形成阶段可从中间步骤中线性解码，且泛化能力强；4. 实验证明，通过识别承诺边界提前结束推理，可平均缩短55%的思维链长度，且模型准确率几乎不受影响。

Conclusion: 研究表明，思维链推理过程存在“承诺边界”现象，模型在推理中途即可确定最终答案，后续步骤多为冗余。基于此，通过识别并提前退出推理过程，可以在几乎不损失性能的前提下，显著缩短推理路径，提升推理效率。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning is the dominant paradigm for inference-time scaling in language models, yet the causal influence of individual steps on the final answer poorly understood. We estimate each step's causal importance via early exit and use this measure to study how answers form across the reasoning traces of several model families. Across diverse tasks, we find that reasoning typically crosses a \emph{commitment boundary} -- a sharp transition from transient intermediate guesses to a stable, high-confidence answer. This transition often happens in a single step, well before the model's reasoning block ends, and is followed by \emph{epiphenomenal} CoT steps that leave the final answer probability unaltered. Using attention probes, we show that answer-formation stages can be linearly decoded from intermediate reasoning steps with high accuracy and generalize robustly to unseen reasoning tasks. We exploit this signal to early-exit reasoning blocks at the commitment boundary, reducing the length of CoTs up to 55\% on average with negligible impact on model performance.

</details>

Abstract: Passive acoustic monitoring holds great promise for ecological inference, yet existing automated tools are typically narrowly trained and non-transferable. Our domain-adapted specialist model outperforms a state-of-the-art general model across all metrics (macro F1: 0.21 vs. 0.07; AUC: 0.74 vs. 0.45; AP: 0.32 vs. 0.19), with active learning further raising F1 to 0.34 and AUC to 0.84. Beyond classification, the learned embeddings encode ecologically meaningful structure, exposed through an interactive visualisation tool for ecological discovery.

*Raphaël Razafindralambo,Rémy Sun,Frédéric Precioso,Jes Frellsen,Pierre-Alexandre Mattei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出“Jeffrey指导”（Jeffrey guidance），这是一种基于Jeffrey条件化规则的扩散模型控制框架。它能在不改变模型基本条件结构的前提下，通过对分布进行最小化扰动，实现对生成目标的高效引导，在提升图像质量和强制属性公平性方面表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散模型指导技术（如分类器引导）通常依赖于启发式能量函数或具体的条件规则，难以处理目标分布不明确或复杂分布约束的问题。作者旨在建立一个更具普适性、更有原则的控制框架，以应对超出传统指导范围的应用场景。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于Jeffrey条件化规则（Jeffrey's rule of conditioning）的新型指导框架。该方法通过更新边缘分布以逼近目标分布，同时保持原有的条件结构，旨在以最小化KL散度的方式对联合分布进行扰动。

Result: 实验证明，该方法在CIFAR-10和FFHQ数据集上利用Inception嵌入作为目标分布，显著降低了FID分数；此外，在CelebA-HQ数据集上，该方法成功地将无条件扩散模型更新为满足属性独立性的公平生成模型。

Conclusion: 本文提出的Jeffrey指导框架为扩散模型提供了一种有原则的、数学上完备的控制方法，能够通过最小化对原始分布的扰动来实现复杂的分布转换任务，在提升图像生成质量和实现公平性约束方面展现了显著的效果。

Abstract: A key strength of diffusion models lies in their flexibility, since their outputs can be controlled at sampling time through guidance. However, beyond simple cases such as conditional sampling, the target distribution is often left implicit, defined only through a sampling rule or a heuristic energy function. To address this, we propose Jeffrey guidance, a principled framework that extends diffusion-model control to applications beyond what standard guidance can express. It leverages Jeffrey's rule of conditioning to update marginal distributions towards a prescribed target, preserving the conditional structure and minimally perturbing the joint distribution. We first demonstrate Jeffrey guidance by targeting a prescribed embedding distribution. With Inception embeddings as the target, this leads to substantial reductions in FID on both CIFAR-10 and FFHQ. We further apply Jeffrey guidance to fairness on CelebA-HQ, updating an unconditional diffusion model to enforce independence between attributes.

</details>

Abstract: To better understand Martian Surface, which is needed to enable Rovers navigate Mars with ease, it is necessary to be able to determine the location of mounds. Detection of mounds was done by manually mapping morphological parameters onto Digital Elevation Models. This paper solves the problem by automatically detecting and or predicting mounds on Mars using Neural Network based Semantic Segmentation methodologies. This is done by using supervised semantic segmentation model and generative adversarial approach. A comparison of the approaches shows that adding extra artificially generated data did not improve the result.

### [163] [Extracting Governing Equations from Latent Dynamics via Multi-View Contrastive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13260)
*Paolo Muratore,Mackenzie Weygandt Mathis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DYSCO是一种利用多视图对比学习从高维带噪观测中识别底层非线性动力系统的新算法，具备强大的噪声抑制能力，并支持动力学方程的符号化恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从带噪、高维观测中识别潜在动力系统是表征学习、系统识别和科学发现的核心挑战。现有方法往往难以有效分离复杂观测中的高维噪声与潜在的底层动力学，尤其是在非线性观测和特定噪声分布（如泊松噪声）的情况下。因此，研究人员寻求一种能够从多视图数据中解耦噪声并恢复稳健动力方程的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为DYSCO的多视图时间对比学习算法。该方法利用同一底层动力过程的多个独立且带噪的视图来区分信号与噪声，结合结构化函数基对动力学进行参数化，从而实现潜在轨迹的恢复和支配方程的符号化提取。此外，该方法通过仿射规范（affine gauge）实现了动力系统的强辨识。

Result: 理论上，该方法提供了在仿射不确定性下的强辨识保证。实证结果表明，无论是在高斯噪声还是泊松噪声环境下，DYSCO均能准确恢复混沌、振荡和亚稳态等多种动力学制度下的潜在轨迹与流场，并能有效提取出底层的支配方程。

Conclusion: DYSCO证明了在多视图观测下，从带噪高维数据中恢复底层动力系统是可行的，并为动力系统的符号化发现提供了一个稳健的框架。其理论保证和实证结果表明，该方法在处理复杂动力学和各种噪声模型（包括生物神经记录中的泊松噪声）方面具有显著优势。

Abstract: Identifying latent dynamical systems from noisy, high-dimensional measurements is a central problem at the intersection of representation learning, system identification, and scientific discovery. We present DYSCO, a multi-view temporal contrastive learning algorithm that jointly recovers latent trajectories and the governing dynamics from such observations, by leveraging multiple independent noisy views of the same underlying process to disentangle signal from noise. By parameterizing the dynamics in a structured functional basis, our framework further enables symbolic recovery of the governing equations within an affine gauge. We offer theoretical guarantees for strong identification up to an affine indeterminacy, extending prior identifiability results to the realistic setting of noisy nonlinear observations. Empirically, we demonstrate accurate recovery of both latent trajectories and flow fields across a diverse set of dynamical regimes (e.g., chaotic, oscillatory, and metastable) under both Gaussian and Poisson observation noise, the latter being particularly relevant for neural recordings.

</details>


### [164] [Different Layers, Different Manifolds: Module-Wise Weight-Space Geometry in Transformer Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13276)
*Kirato Yoshihara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文指出Transformer不同模块对几何约束的偏好不同，提出应为Attention和MLP模块分配不同的流形约束（分别为Stiefel和DGram），以避免训练不稳定并提升整体性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经网路优化通常对所有权重矩阵应用统一的流形约束，但该研究质疑不同Transformer模块是否偏好不同的几何结构，旨在探索更精细化的几何优化策略。

Method: 研究人员在GPT-2预训练任务中应用了“Manifold Muon”算法，对比了将Stiefel和DGram流形约束分配给不同层（Attention模块与MLP模块）的组合效果，并通过分析权重矩阵的奇异值增长情况来诊断训练不稳定性的根源。

Result: 实验发现，将Attention层限制在Stiefel流形上，同时将MLP层限制在DGram流形上，能获得最佳性能；反之，若在Attention层使用DGram约束则会导致奇异值过度增长，引发注意力Logits放大及Softmax饱和，导致训练不稳定。

Conclusion: 研究表明，Transformer模型的优化应当采取模块特异性（module-specific）的几何约束策略，而非统一应用。针对不同模块（Attention与MLP）采用差异化的流形几何（Stiefel vs DGram）能够显著提升训练稳定性与模型性能。

Abstract: Weight-space geometry plays a central role in neural network optimization, yet manifold constraints are often applied uniformly across all weight matrices. In this work, we ask whether different transformer modules prefer different manifold geometries. We study Manifold Muon for GPT-2 pretraining and compare layer-wise assignments of Stiefel and DGram constraints across attention and MLP blocks. Our results show a clear asymmetry: constraining attention layers with Stiefel geometry while assigning DGram geometry to MLP layers gives the best performance among the tested configurations, whereas the inverted assignment and all-DGram configuration become unstable under the shared hyperparameter setting. We trace this failure to singular value growth in DGram-constrained attention weights, which can amplify attention logits and induce softmax saturation. These findings suggest that symmetry-aware and geometry-aware optimization for transformers should be module-specific rather than uniform.

</details>


### [165] [Once-for-All: Scalable Simultaneous Forecasting via Equilibrium State Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13285)
*Beinan Xu,Andy Song,Jiti Gao,Feng Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ESE 提出了一种全新的多系统协同预测范式，通过先估计平衡态再进行预测，在保持高准确度的同时实现了显著的速度提升与线性时间复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常逐个进行系统预测，在处理大规模交互系统（如经济、医疗建模）时效率低下，难以捕捉系统间的协调关系。

Method: 引入平衡态估计 (ESE) 范式，通过单次计算估计系统间的平衡态，并基于当前状态与平衡态的差异生成整体预测；具有线性时间复杂度。

Result: 实验表明 ESE 在保持与当前最优方法 (SOTA) 相当的准确率的同时，实现了 10-70 倍的计算加速，且在系统数量增加时表现出更好的可扩展性和抗扰动性。

Conclusion: ESE 是一种高效、可扩展且稳健的协同预测框架，通过平衡态估计实现了多系统预测的性能与速度的双重提升，特别适用于系统交互复杂的场景。

Abstract: We introduce Equilibrium State Estimation (ESE), a novel paradigm for simultaneous prediction, where multiple interacting systems require separate yet coordinated forecasts. Such scenarios often arise in real-world settings such as economics and healthcare modeling. Unlike existing approaches that predict one system at a time, ESE forecasts all systems in a single pass. It first estimates the equilibrium state across systems, then generates holistic forecasts based on the difference between the current state and the estimated equilibrium. Extensive experiments on synthetic and real-world datasets, including currency exchange and COVID-19 spread modeling, demonstrate that ESE is at least as accurate as state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods while being significantly faster. In addition, ESE integrates seamlessly with conventional predictors, combining their accuracy with its exceptional efficiency and delivering a 10-70x speedup. With linear-time complexity, ESE scales far better than SOTA methods as the number of systems increases. Moreover, it remains accurate under diverse perturbations, establishing ESE as a fast, generalizable, robust, and scalable multi-prediction method.

### [166] [Clipping Makes Distributed and Federated Asynchronous SGD Robust to Stragglers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13287)
*Samuel Erickson,Mikael Johansson*

Main category: cs.LG
